A Generic Report¶

A Subtitle¶

nbprint_contenttableofcontents = nbprint_config.content[1]
nbprint_contenttableofcontents(ctx=nbprint_ctx)

Section One¶

Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet.

Subsection One¶

Consectetur adipiscing elit, sed do eiusmod tempor incididunt.

Subsection Two¶

Ut labore et dolore magna aliqua.

from superstore import superstore
df = superstore()
for i in range(100):
  print(df)
